### [151] [GridProbe: Posterior-Probing for Adaptive Test-Time Compute in Long-Video VLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10762v1)
*Mohamed Eltahir,Lama Ayash,Ali Habibullah,Tanveer Hussain,Naeemullah Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 自适应测试时计算，动态选择推理帧，可迁移至agent的规划与资源分配

TL;DR: GridProbe通过后验探针和形状自适应选择，在长视频理解中实现高效、自适应的帧选择，降低计算成本且几乎不损失准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长视频理解在VLM中受限于单个大规模前向传播和二次注意力成本，现有免训练帧选择方法在推理密集型查询上表现不佳。

Method: 将帧排列成K×K网格，运行轻量级行和列探针，读取峰值后验作为置信度，外积生成重要性图，利用偏度和峰度进行形状自适应选择，动态确定每问题的有效帧预算Meff。

Result: 在Video-MME-v2上以3.36倍TFLOPs减少达到1.6百分点内准确率；在LongVideoBench上以0.35倍计算量提升0.9百分点；解耦选择器与QA模型后，2B+8B组合在0.52倍计算量下平均提升4.0百分点。

Conclusion: GridProbe实现了测试时自适应计算和可解释性，为长视频理解的高效推理和未来研究方向提供了新范式。

中文摘要：在视觉语言模型（VLM）中，长视频理解受到单个大规模前向传播的瓶颈，该传播需要对数千帧进行二次注意力成本计算。一种常见的缓解方法是在前向传播之前首先选择一小部分信息丰富的帧；通常通过辅助编码器空间相似性进行免训练选择。然而，这种信号受到对比预训练的限制，通常在推理密集型查询（否定、跨帧计数、整体总结）上失败。我们提出GridProbe，一种高效的免训练后验探针推理范式，它使用冻结的VLM自身的推理在答案空间中为证据评分，然后自适应地选择与问题相关的帧，从而实现次二次注意力成本，几乎不损失准确性。我们将帧排列在$K{\times}K$的网格上，并运行轻量级的行R和列C探针，其中每个探针将其峰值后验作为查询条件置信度读取。R和C的外积产生一个可解释的重要性图，其偏度和峰度驱动形状自适应选择，这是一个闭式规则，可靠地将固定帧预算$M$替换为每个问题的$M_{\mathrm{eff}}$。我们经验性地证明，$M_{\mathrm{eff}}$在从未见过答案的情况下跟踪内在问题难度，这是测试时自适应计算的一个标志。在Video-MME-v2上，GridProbe与整体基线在平均准确率上相差1.6个百分点内，同时减少了3.36倍TFLOPs；而在LongVideoBench上，它Pareto支配了基线（在0.35倍计算量下提高了0.9个百分点）。由于选择器和问答模型可以解耦，将一个小型2B选择器与更强的4B或8B问答模型配对，严格Pareto优于2B整体基线（平均在0.52倍计算量下提高多达4.0个百分点），且无需重新训练。最后，重要性图的可解释性为行为诊断、基础性和帧选择蒸馏开辟了未来途径。

Original abstract: Long-video understanding in VLMs is bottlenecked by a single monolithic forward pass over thousands of frames at quadratic attention cost. A common mitigation is to first select a small subset of informative frames before the forward pass; common for training-free selectors via auxiliary encoder-space similarities. Such signals are capped by contrastive pretraining, which usually fails on reasoning-heavy queries (negation, cross-frame counting, holistic summarization). We propose GridProbe, an efficient training-free posterior-probing inference paradigm that scores evidence in answer space using a frozen VLM's own reasoning and then selects question-relevant frames adaptively, resulting in sub-quadratic attention cost with little to no accuracy loss. We arrange frames on a $K{\times}K$ grid and run lightweight row R and column C probes, where each probe reads its peak posterior as a query-conditioned confidence. The outer product of R and C yields an interpretable importance map whose skewness and kurtosis drive Shape-Adaptive Selection, a closed-form rule that reliably replaces the fixed frame budget $M$ with a per-question $M_{\mathrm{eff}}$. We show empirically that $M_{\mathrm{eff}}$ tracks intrinsic question difficulty without ever seeing the answer, a sign of test-time adaptive compute. On Video-MME-v2, GridProbe matches the monolithic baseline within $1.6$ pp Avg Acc at $3.36\times$ TFLOPs reduction, while on LongVideoBench it Pareto-dominates the baseline ($+0.9$ pp at $0.35\times$ compute). Because the selector and QA models can be decoupled, pairing a small 2B selector with a stronger 4B or 8B QA is strictly Pareto-dominant over the 2B monolithic baseline (up to $+4.0$ pp at $0.52\times$ compute, on average), with no retraining. Finally, the interpretability of the importance maps opens future avenues for behavioral diagnostics, grounding, and frame-selection distillation.

</details>


### [152] [Break the Brake, Not the Wheel: Untargeted Jailbreak via Entropy Maximization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10764v3)
*Mengqi He,Xinyu Tian,Xin Shen,Shu Zou,Jinhong Ni,Zhaoyuan Yang,Weikang Li,Xuesong Li,Jing Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: VLM越狱攻击，涉及LLM安全，可迁移至agent安全防护

TL;DR: 通过最大化决策令牌熵的轻量级攻击UJEM-KL，实现了视觉语言模型上具有跨模型迁移性的无目标越狱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有梯度通用图像越狱缺乏跨模型迁移性，且拒绝行为集中于高熵令牌，非拒绝令牌已有较高概率，因此可通过熵最大化翻转拒绝。

Method: 提出UJEM-KL，在自回归解码的关键高熵令牌上最大化熵以消除拒绝，同时稳定低熵位置保持输出质量。

Result: 在三个VLM和两个安全基准上，白盒攻击成功率竞争且迁移性提高，对抗防御有效，表明有限迁移性源于过约束优化。

Conclusion: 通过放松优化约束，利用熵最大化可实现可迁移的无目标越狱，揭示了迁移性受限的根本原因。

中文摘要：近期研究表明，基于梯度的通用图像越狱对视觉语言模型（VLM）表现出很少或没有跨模型迁移性，这使人们对可迁移多模态越狱的可行性产生了质疑。我们在严格无目标威胁模型下重新审视这一结论，不强制执行固定前缀或响应模式。我们的初步实验揭示，在自回归解码过程中，拒绝行为集中出现在高熵令牌上，而在攻击之前，非拒绝令牌在排名靠前的候选者中已经占据了相当大的概率质量。受此发现启发，我们提出了通过熵最大化的无目标越狱（UJEM）-KL，这是一种轻量级攻击，通过最大化这些决策令牌的熵来翻转拒绝结果，同时稳定剩余的低熵位置以保持输出质量。在三个VLM和两个安全基准上，UJEM-KL实现了具有竞争力的白盒攻击成功率，并持续提高了可迁移性，同时在代表性防御下仍然有效。我们的实验结果表明，有限的迁移性主要源于过度约束的优化目标。

Original abstract: Recent studies show that gradient-based universal image jailbreaks on vision-language models (VLMs) exhibit little or no cross-model transferability, casting doubt on the feasibility of transferable multimodal jailbreaks. We revisit this conclusion under a strictly untargeted threat model without enforcing a fixed prefix or response pattern. Our preliminary experiment reveals that refusal behavior concentrates at high-entropy tokens during autoregressive decoding, and non-refusal tokens already carry substantial probability mass among the top-ranked candidates before attack. Motivated by this finding, we propose Untargeted Jailbreak via Entropy Maximization(UJEM)-KL, a lightweight attack that maximizes entropy at these decision tokens to flip refusal outcomes, while stabilizing the remaining low-entropy positions to preserve output quality. Across three VLMs and two safety benchmarks, UJEM-KL achieves competitive white-box attack success rates and consistently improves transferability, while remaining effective under representative defenses. Our experimental results indicate that the limited transferability primarily stems from overly constrained optimization objectives.

</details>


### [153] [Dynamic Cross-Modal Prompt Generation for Multimodal Continual Instruction Tuning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10765v1)
*Tao Hu,Da-Wei Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 动态提示生成用于持续微调，prompt学习方法可迁移至agent

TL;DR: 提出动态跨模态提示生成框架DRAPE，通过实例级自适应软提示和遗忘缓解机制，在多模态持续指令微调中达到最先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖任务级模块，无法适应同一任务内样本在视觉场景、意图和推理需求上的差异，需要实例级适应。

Method: 构建DRAPE框架，从文本指令派生提示查询，与视觉特征交叉注意力生成实例特定软提示；采用零空间梯度投影和CLIP原型路由分别缓解遗忘和实现无任务标签的生成器选择。

Result: 在MCIT基准上，DRAPE在基于提示和LoRA的持续学习基线中取得最先进性能。

Conclusion: DRAPE通过实例级动态提示和遗忘缓解策略，有效解决多模态持续指令微调中的适应与遗忘问题，性能领先。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）通过指令微调取得了强大性能，但在实际部署中通常需要跨连续任务不断扩展能力。在这种场景下，多模态持续指令微调（MCIT）旨在获取新能力的同时限制灾难性遗忘。现有方法主要遵循模块组合范式：它们维护任务级提示或LoRA专家，并在推理时动态路由或聚合其中一部分。然而，同一任务内的样本在视觉场景、问题意图和推理需求方面仍然可能存在显著差异。这促使我们进行实例级适应，针对单个查询-图像对，而不仅选择或组合任务级模块。为此，我们提出了DRAPE（动态跨模态提示生成），这是一个提示学习框架，为MCIT合成连续的实例特定软提示。DRAPE不从固定池中选择提示，而是从文本指令中派生提示查询，并与视觉补丁特征进行交叉注意力，生成查询-图像条件化的提示，这些提示被前置到冻结的LLM。为了减轻顺序更新中的遗忘，DRAPE对共享投影器应用零空间梯度投影，并在推理时使用基于CLIP的原型路由进行无任务标签的生成器选择。在MCIT基准上的大量实验表明，DRAPE在代表性的基于提示和基于LoRA的持续学习基线中取得了最先进的性能。

Original abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) achieve strong performance through instruction tuning, yet real-world deployment often requires continual capability expansion across sequential tasks. In such scenarios, Multimodal Continual Instruction Tuning (MCIT) aims to acquire new capabilities while limiting catastrophic forgetting. Existing methods mainly follow a module-composition paradigm: they maintain task-level prompts or LoRA experts and dynamically route or aggregate a subset of them at inference. However, samples within the same task can still differ substantially in visual scenes, question intents, and reasoning demands. This motivates instance-level adaptation to individual query-image pairs rather than only selecting or combining task-level modules. To this end, we propose DRAPE (Dynamic Cross-Modal Prompt Generation), a prompt-learning framework that synthesizes continuous instance-specific soft prompts for MCIT. Instead of selecting prompts from a fixed pool, DRAPE derives prompt queries from the textual instruction and cross-attends to visual patch features, producing query-image conditioned prompts that are prepended to the frozen LLM. To mitigate forgetting during sequential updates, DRAPE applies null-space gradient projection to the shared projector and uses CLIP-based prototype routing for task-label-free generator selection at inference. Extensive experiments on MCIT benchmarks show that DRAPE achieves state-of-the-art performance among representative prompt-based and LoRA-based continual-learning baselines.

</details>


### [154] [CADBench: A Multimodal Benchmark for AI-Assisted CAD Program Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10873v2)
*Anna C. Doris,Jacob Thomas Sony,Ghadi Nehme,Era Syla,Amin Heyrani Nobari,Faez Ahmed*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: CAD程序生成benchmark，涉及代码生成agent，可迁移

TL;DR: CADBench是一个统一的多模态CAD程序生成基准，包含18000个样本、五种输入模态和六种指标，评估了11个系统，揭示了专用网格到CAD模型优于通用VLM但存在三种失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估碎片化，难以衡量从图像或3D观测中恢复可编辑CAD程序的进展，因此需要统一基准。

Method: 构建了包含18000个样本的CADBench基准，涵盖六个基准族、五种输入模态（干净网格、噪声网格、单视图渲染、照片级渲染、多视图渲染）和六种指标（几何保真度、可执行性、程序紧凑性等），对11个CAD专用和通用视觉语言系统进行大规模基准测试。

Result: 在理想输入下，专用网格到CAD模型显著优于代码生成VLM；重建质量随几何复杂度下降，模型在模态变化下表现脆弱，且模型排名因指标而异。

Conclusion: CADBench作为诊断测试平台，能够有效衡量可编辑3D重建和多模态CAD理解的进展，并揭示现有方法的不足。

中文摘要：从图像或3D观测中恢复可编辑的CAD程序是AI辅助设计的核心，但由于现有评估分散在不同的数据集、模态和指标上，进展难以衡量。我们提出CADBench，一个用于多模态CAD程序生成的统一基准。CADBench包含来自DeepCAD、Fusion 360、ABC、MCB和Objaverse的六个基准族的18000个评估样本；五种输入模态，包括干净网格、噪声网格、单视图渲染、照片级渲染和多视图渲染；以及六种指标，涵盖几何保真度、可执行性和程序紧凑性。基于STEP的族按B-rep面数分层，所有族通过多样性采样以支持跨复杂度和对象变化的可控分析。我们对11个专用CAD和通用视觉语言系统进行基准测试，生成了超过140万个CAD程序。在理想化输入下，专用网格到CAD模型显著优于代码生成的视觉语言模型，后者仍远未实现可靠的CAD程序重建。CADBench进一步揭示了三种常见的失败模式：重建质量随几何复杂度下降、专用CAD模型在模态变化下脆弱、以及模型排名随指标变化。这些结果共同将CADBench定位为衡量可编辑3D重建和多模态CAD理解进展的诊断性测试平台。该基准公开于https://github.com/anniedoris/CADBench。

Original abstract: Recovering editable CAD programs from images or 3D observations is central to AI-assisted design, but progress is difficult to measure because existing evaluations are fragmented across datasets, modalities, and metrics. We introduce CADBench, a unified benchmark for multimodal CAD program generation. CADBench contains 18,000 evaluation samples spanning six benchmark families derived from DeepCAD, Fusion 360, ABC, MCB, and Objaverse; five input modalities including clean meshes, noisy meshes, single-view renders, photorealistic renders, and multi-view renders; and six metrics covering geometric fidelity, executability, and program compactness. STEP-based families are stratified by B-rep face count and all families are diversity-sampled to support controlled analysis across complexity and object variation. We benchmark eleven CAD-specialized and general-purpose vision-language systems, generating more than 1.4 million CAD programs. Under idealized inputs, specialized mesh-to-CAD models substantially outperform code-generating VLMs, which remain far from reliable CAD program reconstruction. CADBench further reveals three recurring failure modes: reconstruction quality degrades with geometric complexity, CAD-specialized models can be brittle under modality shift, and model rankings change across metrics. Together, these results position CADBench as a diagnostic testbed for measuring progress in editable 3D reconstruction and multimodal CAD understanding. The benchmark is publicly available at https://github.com/anniedoris/CADBench.

</details>


### [155] [ABRA: Agent Benchmark for Radiology Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11224v1)
*Bulat Maksudov,Vladislav Kurenkov,Kathleen M. Curran,Alessandra Mileo*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 放射科agent benchmark，含通用工具调用与评分架构，可迁移至其他agent。

TL;DR: ABRA是一个放射学智能体基准，通过函数调用工具模拟DICOM环境，发现当前模型在感知方面存在瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医疗智能体基准将影像作为预选样本，缺乏智能体需要导航的真实环境，因此需要新的基准来评估放射学智能体的能力。

Method: 构建了ABRA基准，包含21个函数调用工具，655个程序化生成任务，覆盖多种类型和难度，并使用自动评分器评估Planning、Execution和Outcome。

Result: 模型在真实标注上Execution高但Outcome低（0-25%），而预言机变体下Outcome达69-100%，表明瓶颈在于感知而非工具协调。

Conclusion: 当前模型在工具执行方面表现良好，但感知能力不足，未来需提升模型对影像的理解和检测能力。

中文摘要：现有的医疗智能体基准将影像作为预选样本提供，而非智能体必须导航的环境。我们提出ABRA，一个放射学智能体基准，其中智能体通过二十一个函数调用工具操作OHIF查看器和Orthanc DICOM服务器，这些工具涵盖切片导航、窗宽窗位调整、序列选择、像素坐标标注和结构化报告。ABRA包含655个程序化生成的任务，涵盖三个难度层级和八种类型（查看器控制、元数据问答、视觉探针、标注、纵向比较、BI-RADS报告，以及标注和BI-RADS报告的预言机变体），数据来自LIDC-IDRI、杜克乳腺癌MRI和NLST新病灶LongCT。每次任务根据Planning、Execution和Outcome（Bluethgen等，2025）由特定任务类型的自动评分器评分。十个当前模型（五个闭源权重和五个开源权重）在真实标注上达到至少89%的Execution，但仅0-25%的Outcome；在配对预言机变体中，模拟检测器提供发现，相同任务的Outcome在所有评估模型上达到69-100%，将瓶颈定位于感知而非工具协调。代码、任务生成器和评分器发布在https://github.com/Luab/ABRA

Original abstract: Existing medical-agent benchmarks deliver imaging as pre-selected samples, never as an environment the agent must navigate. We introduce ABRA, a radiology-agent benchmark in which the agent operates an OHIF viewer and an Orthanc DICOM server through twenty-one function-calling tools that span slice navigation, windowing, series selection, pixel-coordinate annotation, and structured reporting. ABRA contains 655 programmatically generated tasks across three difficulty tiers and eight types (viewer control, metadata QA, vision probe, annotation, longitudinal comparison, BI-RADS reporting, and oracle variants of annotation and BI-RADS reporting), drawn from LIDC-IDRI, Duke Breast Cancer MRI, and NLST New-Lesion LongCT. Each episode is scored along Planning, Execution, and Outcome (Bluethgen et al., 2025) by task-type-specific automatic scorers. Ten current models, five closed-weight and five open-weight, reach at least 89% Execution on real annotation but only 0-25% Outcome; on the paired oracle variant where a simulated detector supplies the finding, Outcome on the same task reaches 69-100% across the models evaluated, localising the bottleneck to perception rather than tool orchestration. Code, task generators, and scorers are released at https://github.com/Luab/ABRA

</details>

### [156] [GraphInstruct: A Progressive Benchmark for Diagnosing Capability Gaps in LLM Graph Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.09997v2)
*Zihe Wei,Sheng Xiang,Ying Zhang,Changjun Jiang*

Main category: cs.SI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了GraphInstruct基准，通过六个复杂度级别和五个评估维度系统评估LLM的图生成能力，发现多约束组合是关键瓶颈，并验证了验证引导迭代框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图生成基准未考虑LLM时代指令跟随需求，且按类型或任务域划分无法定位模型在复杂度谱系中的具体失效点。

Method: 构建GraphInstruct基准，包含六个复杂度级别、五个评估维度、800条指令和1,582个参考解，评估12个LLM在45种配置下的表现，并提出验证引导迭代框架。

Result: 区分能力峰值出现在多约束组合而非推理深度；无单一提示策略占优；领域语义约束迭代不变；验证引导框架超越提示工程上限。

Conclusion: 图生成任务中，检索比额外计算更关键，细粒度基准信号能有效指导方法开发。

中文摘要：图结构化数据支撑着从引文分析和社交网络建模到分子设计和知识图谱构建等应用，大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被用作提示驱动的图合成器。经典的图生成综述回顾了深度生成模型及其评估基础，但早于LLM时代，并未为评估指令跟随的图合成提供基础。最近的LLM时代基准沿着图类型或任务域轴评估模型；然而，这种组织方式平均化了结构复杂性，无法定位LLM在复杂性谱系中何处失效。为了弥补这一诊断空白，我们引入了GraphInstruct，一个渐进复杂度的基准，将LLM图生成分层为六个复杂度级别和五个评估维度，并配有800条手工编写的指令、1,582个算法合成的参考解，以及跨越45个（模型，策略）配置的12个LLM能力评估。我们发现，区分能力在多约束组合上达到峰值，而非推理深度；没有单一的提示策略在级别或模型家族中占主导地位；并且领域语义约束在所有测试方法下保持迭代不变——这表明检索而非额外计算是下一个研究前沿。在基准之上，一个带有约束感知自适应提示的验证引导迭代框架始终超越测试目标模型上的提示工程上限，表明基准的细粒度信号驱动方法发展。数据和代码以及可复现性工件随论文一同发布在https://github.com/AI4DataSynth/GraphInstruct_formal。

Original abstract: Graph-structured data underpins applications from citation analysis and social-network modeling to molecular design and knowledge-graph construction, and Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used as prompt-driven graph synthesizers. Classical graph-generation reviews catalog deep generative models and their evaluation primitives, but predate the LLM era and provide no foundation for evaluating instruction-following graph synthesis. Recent LLM-era benchmarks evaluate models along graph-type or task-domain axes; such organizations, however, average over structural complexity and cannot localize where in the complexity spectrum an LLM breaks down. To close this diagnostic gap, we introduce GraphInstruct, a progressive-complexity benchmark that stratifies LLM graph generation into six complexity levels and five evaluation dimensions, paired with 800 hand-authored instructions, 1,582 algorithmically synthesized reference solutions, and a 12-LLM capability evaluation across 45 (model, strategy) configurations. We find that discriminative power peaks at multi-constraint composition rather than reasoning depth, that no single prompting strategy dominates across levels or model families, and that domain-semantic constraints remain iteration-invariant under all tested methods -- pointing to retrieval rather than additional compute as the next research frontier. Atop the benchmark, a verification-guided iterative framework with constraint-aware adaptive prompting consistently surpasses the prompt-engineering ceiling on tested target models, demonstrating that the benchmark's fine-grained signals drive method development. Data, code, and reproducibility artifacts are released alongside the paper at https://github.com/AI4DataSynth/GraphInstruct_formal

</details>

# cs.RO [[Back]](#toc)

### [157] [Retrieve-then-Steer: Online Success Memory for Test-Time Adaptation of Generative VLAs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10094v2)
*Jianchao Zhao,Huoren Yang,Yusong Hu,Yuyang Gao,Qiguan Ou,Cong Wan,SongLin Dong,Zhiheng Ma,Yihong Gong*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 机器人VLA的在线成功记忆测试时自适应，涉及记忆复用和检索，可迁移到coding agent经验复用。

TL;DR: 提出一种在线成功记忆引导的测试时自适应框架，通过重用成功经验提升冻结VLA模型的闭环可靠性，无需参数更新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估将测试视为零次独立尝试，但现实机器人常在重复或缓慢变化环境中运行，成功执行提供了可靠行为模式的证据。研究能否通过重用测试时经验提升部分胜任的冻结VLA的可靠性。

Method: 提出在线成功记忆引导的测试时自适应框架，包括存储进度校准成功片段、检索状态相关动作块、通过轨迹一致性过滤并聚合为精英动作先验，以及置信度自适应先验引导注入到流匹配动作采样器。

Result: 模拟和真实世界实验显示任务成功率和闭环稳定性提升，尤其在长时域和多阶段任务中。

Conclusion: 该检索-引导机制实现了轻量级非参数测试时自适应，无需参数更新，显著提升性能。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在通用机器人操作方面展现出巨大潜力，但其闭环可靠性在本地部署条件下往往会下降。现有评估通常将测试回合视为独立的零次尝试。然而，现实机器人常常在同一或缓慢变化的环境中重复运行，成功的执行为可靠的行为模式提供了经过环境验证的证据。我们研究了这种持续部署设置，探讨一个部分胜任的冻结VLA是否可以通过重用其成功的测试时经验来提高可靠性。我们提出了一种针对生成式VLA的在线成功记忆引导的测试时自适应框架。在部署期间，机器人将进度校准的成功观察-动作片段存储在长期记忆中。在推理时，它检索与状态相关的动作块，通过轨迹级一致性过滤不一致的候选者，并将它们聚合为精英动作先验。为了将这个先验融入动作生成，我们引入了置信度自适应先验引导，它将精英先验注入到流匹配动作采样器的中间状态，并根据检索置信度调整引导强度。这种设计允许冻结的VLA利用特定环境的成功经验，同时保留基于观察的条件生成细化。这种检索-引导机制实现了轻量级、非参数的测试时自适应，无需参数更新。模拟和真实世界实验表明，任务成功率和闭环稳定性得到提升，特别是在长时域和多阶段任务中。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models show strong potential for general-purpose robotic manipulation, yet their closed-loop reliability often degrades under local deployment conditions. Existing evaluations typically treat test episodes as independent zero-shot trials. However, real robots often operate repeatedly in the same or slowly changing environments, where successful executions provide environment-verified evidence of reliable behavior patterns. We study this persistent-deployment setting, asking whether a partially competent frozen VLA can improve its reliability by reusing its successful test-time experience. We propose an online success-memory guided test-time adaptation framework for generative VLAs. During deployment, the robot stores progress-calibrated successful observation-action segments in a long-term memory. At inference, it retrieves state-relevant action chunks, filters inconsistent candidates via trajectory-level consistency, and aggregates them into an elite action prior. To incorporate this prior into action generation, we introduce confidence-adaptive prior guidance, which injects the elite prior into an intermediate state of the flow-matching action sampler and adjusts the guidance strength based on retrieval confidence. This design allows the frozen VLA to exploit environment-specific successful experience while preserving observation-conditioned generative refinement. This retrieve-then-steer mechanism enables lightweight, non-parametric test-time adaptation without requiring parameter updates. Simulation and real-world experiments show improved task success and closed-loop stability, especially in long-horizon and multi-stage tasks.

</details>
